<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:размазать.html>разма́зать</a> (18719)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">раз-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">raz-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мазать.html>ма́зать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mázatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:размазать.html>разма́зать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razmázatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:размазывать.html>разма́зывать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to spread
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мальчик.html>ма́льчик</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:размазать.html>разма́зал</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:грязь.html>грязь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>всему́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:лицо.html>лицу́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">málʹčik <b>razmázal</b> grjazʹ po vsemú licú</i> ― <span class="e-translation">a boy spread dirt all over his face</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:размазать.html>разма́зать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:стенка.html>сте́нке</a> кого́-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>razmázatʹ</b> po sténke kovó-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">1) to haul smb over the coals; give smb the works 2) crush smb, make smb bite the dust</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to pad out, to spin out
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:размазать.html>разма́зал</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:свое.html>свой</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:доклад.html>докла́д</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">on <b>razmázal</b> svoj doklád</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he padded out his report</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:размазывать.html>разма́зывать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razmázyvatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:размазать.html>разма́зать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to spread</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to pad out, to spin out</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">разма́хиваться</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">razmáxivatʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="None mention" lang="ru">-∅</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-∅</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span><sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:размах.html>разма́х</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razmáx</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:размах.html>разма́ха</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:размах.html>разма́хи</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:размах.html>разма́хов</a></b>)

<ol><li>swing</li>
<li>sweep
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:со.html>со</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>всего́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:размах.html>разма́ху</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">so vsevó razmáxu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">with all one's might</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ударить.html>уда́рить</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:размах.html>разма́ху</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">udáritʹ s razmáxu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to strike with all one's might</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>wingspread, wingspan</li>
<li><i>(of activity)</i> scope, range, sweep, scale
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:человек.html>челове́к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:широкий.html>широ́кого</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:размах.html>разма́ха</a></b></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">čelovék širókovo <b>razmáxa</b></i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">a man of wide-ranging enterprise</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:приобретать.html>приобрета́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>всё</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:больший.html>бо́льший</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:размах.html>разма́х</a></b></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">priobretátʹ vsjó bólʹšij <b>razmáx</b></i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">to continually gain in scope</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:широкий.html>широ́кий</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:размах.html>разма́х</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:строительство.html>строи́тельства</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">širókij <b>razmáx</b> stroítelʹstva</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">wide scope of construction</span></dd></dl></div></dd>

***размахивать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:размахивать.html>разма́хивать</a> (4264)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">размахну́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">razmaxnútʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ивать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:размахивать.html>разма́хивать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razmáxivatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">размахну́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to sway, to swing</li>
<li>to dangle</li>
<li>to brandish</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">размахну́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">razmaxnútʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

***разменять.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:разменять.html>разменя́ть</a> (20072)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">раз-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">raz-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:менять.html>меня́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">menjátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разменять.html>разменя́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razmenjátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">разме́нивать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to change, to break <i>(money for lesser units)</i></li>
<li>to exchange</li>
<li>to live to certain age
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:разменять.html>разменя́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:четвертый.html>четвёртый</a>/<a href = vnd.unilang:пятый.html>пя́тый</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:десяток.html>деся́ток</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>razmenjátʹ</b> četvjortyj/pjátyj desjátok</i> ― <span class="e-translation">enter one's thirties/forties; be on the wrong side of thirty/forty</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">chess</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to exchange</li></ol>

***разместить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:разместить.html>размести́ть</a> (8028)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">раз-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">raz-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-мести́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-mestítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разместить.html>размести́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razmestítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:размещать.html>размеща́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to place, to put, to stow
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:разместить.html>размести́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:заказ.html>зака́з</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>razmestítʹ</b> zakáz</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to place an order</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:разместить.html>размести́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:реклама.html>рекла́му</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>razmestítʹ</b> reklámu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to advertise); put up an advertisement</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to accommodate, to put up, to house, to quarter, to billet
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:разместить.html>размести́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:гостиница.html>гости́нице</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>razmestítʹ</b> v gostínice</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to provide with hotel accommodation; put up in a hotel</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>вы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мочь.html>мо́жете</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:разместить.html>размести́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>нас</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>себя́</a>?</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">vy móžete <b>razmestítʹ</b> nas u sebjá?</i> ― <span class="e-translation">can you put us up (at your place)?</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:разместить.html>размести́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:пострадавший.html>пострада́вших</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:наводнение.html>наводне́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:школа.html>шко́ле</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>razmestítʹ</b> postradávšix ot navodnénija v škóle</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to house flood victims in a school</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to deploy, to station
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:разместить.html>размести́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:войско.html>войска</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>razmestítʹ</b> vojska</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to deploy/station troops</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:разместить.html>размести́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ракета.html>раке́ты</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>razmestítʹ</b> rakéty</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to deploy missiles</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">finance</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to invest, to place
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:разместить.html>размести́ть</a></b> заём</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>razmestítʹ</b> zajóm</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to distribute/float a loan</span></div></dd>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">раз-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">raz-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:метать.html>мета́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">metátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разметать.html>размета́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razmetátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">размётывать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to destroy</li>
<li>to scatter</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to spread apart</li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:размещать.html>размеща́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razmeščátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разместить.html>размести́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to place, to put, to stow
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:размещать.html>размеща́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:заказ.html>зака́з</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>razmeščátʹ</b> zakáz</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to place an order</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:размещать.html>размеща́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:реклама.html>рекла́му</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>razmeščátʹ</b> reklámu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to advertise); put up an advertisement</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to accommodate, to put up, to house, to quarter, to billet
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:размещать.html>размеща́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:гостиница.html>гости́нице</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>razmeščátʹ</b> v gostínice</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to provide with hotel accommodation; put up in a hotel</span></div></dd></dl></li>

***размещение.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:размещение.html>размеще́ние</a> (12352)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разместить.html>размести́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">razmestítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е́ние</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-énije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:размещение.html>размеще́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razmeščénije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:размещение.html>размеще́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:размещение.html>размеще́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:размещение.html>размеще́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>placing, placement
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:размещение.html>размеще́ние</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мебель.html>ме́бели</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>razmeščénije</b> mébeli</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the placement of furniture</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:размещение.html>размеще́ние</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:груз.html>гру́за</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>razmeščénije</b> grúza</i> ― <span class="e-translation">stowage</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>accommodation
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:номер.html>но́мер</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> одноме́стным (двухме́стным) <b><a href = vnd.unilang:размещение.html>размеще́нием</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">nómer s odnoméstnym (dvuxméstnym) <b>razmeščénijem</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">single (double) room</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:размещение.html>размеще́ние</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:квартира.html>кварти́рам</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:войско.html>во́йск</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>razmeščénije</b> po kvartíram (vojsk)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">quartering; billeting</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>deployment, stationing
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:размещение.html>размеще́ние</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:вооруженный.html>вооружённых</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сила.html>си́л</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>razmeščénije</b> vooružónnyx sil</i> ― <span class="e-translation">deployment/stationing of armed forces</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:размещение.html>размеще́ние</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ракета.html>раке́т</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>razmeščénije</b> rakét</i> ― <span class="e-translation">deployment of missiles</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>placement, layout; distribution pattern
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:размещение.html>размеще́ние</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:население.html>населе́ния</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>razmeščénije</b> naselénija</i> ― <span class="e-translation">population distribution</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:размещение.html>размеще́ние</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:предприятие.html>предприя́тий</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>razmeščénije</b> predprijátij</i> ― <span class="e-translation">placement/distribution of enterprises</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">finances</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> placement
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:размещение.html>размеще́ние</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:капитал.html>капита́ла</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>razmeščénije</b> kapitála</i> ― <span class="e-translation">investment</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:размещение.html>размеще́ние</a></b> за́йма</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>razmeščénije</b> zájma</i> ― <span class="e-translation">distributing/floating a loan</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:размещение.html>размеще́ние</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ценный.html>це́нных</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:бумага.html>бума́г</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>razmeščénije</b> cénnyx bumág</i> ― <span class="e-translation">placement of securities</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:начальный.html>нача́льное</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:публичный.html>публи́чное</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:размещение.html>размеще́ние</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">načálʹnoje publíčnoje <b>razmeščénije</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">initial public offering (IPO)</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
